<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>
<s> he was thus seated twiddling the queer manuscript in his hand joking grimly to himself when his servant came in with a card from a gentleman who wished to speak to him very particularly <\s>
<s> and if pen had gone out into the passage he would have seen sucking his stick rolling his eyes and showing great marks of anxiety his old acquaintance mr <\s>
<s> huxter on particular business <\s>
<s> huxter to come in said pen amused rather and not the less so when poor sam appeared before him <\s>
<s> pray take a chair mr <\s>
<s> huxter said pen in his most superb manner <\s>

<s> i'm in a fix said mr <\s>
<s> she sent me to you continued the young surgeon <\s>

<s> pendennis both of the borough and the lady sir <\s>

<s> and tell him what <\s>

<s> you you don't mean to say you have you have done any wrong to that dear little creature sir <\s>
<s> said pen starting up in a great fury <\s>

<s> pen remembered that blanche had written and mentioned her visit <\s>
<s> i was called in huxter said <\s>
<s> i was in the inn looking after old cos's leg and about something else too very likely and i met strong who told me there was a woman taken ill in chambers and went up to give her my professional services <\s>
<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>
<s> she was taken with strong hysterics i found her kicking and screaming like a good one in strong's chamber along with him and colonel altamont and miss amory crying and as pale as a sheet and altamont fuming about a regular kick up <\s>
<s> they were two hours in the chambers and the old woman went whooping off in a cab <\s>
<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> but it's done and can't be undone and we must make the best of it she has known the story for a month thought pen with a sharp pang of grief and a gloomy sympathy this accounts for her letter of to day <\s>

<s> do you know who altamont is sir <\s>
<s> asked huxter after the pause during which pen had been thinking of his own affairs <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>
<s> he was thus seated twiddling the queer manuscript in his hand joking grimly to himself when his servant came in with a card from a gentleman who wished to speak to him very particularly <\s>
<s> and if pen had gone out into the passage he would have seen sucking his stick rolling his eyes and showing great marks of anxiety his old acquaintance mr <\s>
<s> huxter on particular business <\s>
<s> huxter to come in said pen amused rather and not the less so when poor sam appeared before him <\s>
<s> pray take a chair mr <\s>
<s> huxter said pen in his most superb manner <\s>

<s> i had rather not speak before the flunk before the man mr <\s>

<s> arthur's attendant quitted the room <\s>
<s> i'm in a fix said mr <\s>
<s> she sent me to you continued the young surgeon <\s>
<s> i was coming to see her but i have had a great deal of business since my return to london <\s>

<s> i wish you joy mr <\s>
<s> pendennis both of the borough and the lady sir <\s>

<s> and tell him what <\s>

<s> you you don't mean to say you have you have done any wrong to that dear little creature sir <\s>
<s> said pen starting up in a great fury <\s>
<s> i hope not said huxter with a hangdog look but i've married her <\s>
<s> and i know there will be an awful shindy at home <\s>

<s> but i would have it confound it <\s>
<s> it's all over now and the old boy's wrote me that he's coming up to town for drugs he will be here to morrow and then it must all come out <\s>

<s> pen remembered that blanche had written and mentioned her visit <\s>
<s> i was called in huxter said <\s>
<s> i was in the inn looking after old cos's leg and about something else too very likely and i met strong who told me there was a woman taken ill in chambers and went up to give her my professional services <\s>
<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>
<s> she was taken with strong hysterics i found her kicking and screaming like a good one in strong's chamber along with him and colonel altamont and miss amory crying and as pale as a sheet and altamont fuming about a regular kick up <\s>
<s> they were two hours in the chambers and the old woman went whooping off in a cab <\s>
<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> but it's done and can't be undone and we must make the best of it she has known the story for a month thought pen with a sharp pang of grief and a gloomy sympathy this accounts for her letter of to day <\s>
<s> she will not implicate her father or divulge his secret she wishes to let me off from the marriage and finds a pretext the generous girl <\s>
<s> do you know who altamont is sir <\s>
<s> asked huxter after the pause during which pen had been thinking of his own affairs <\s>

<s> the wife takes the husband's rank of course said pen <\s>

<s> old bows taught her <\s>
<s> and she'll do on the stage if the governor was to throw me over but i'd rather not have her there <\s>

<s> it's what bows says if there were twenty men in a room and one not taking notice of her she wouldn't be satisfied until the twentieth was at her elbow <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>

<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> pen remembered that blanche had written and mentioned her visit <\s>
<s> i was called in huxter said <\s>
<s> i was in the inn looking after old cos's leg and about something else too very likely and i met strong who told me there was a woman taken ill in chambers and went up to give her my professional services <\s>
<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>
<s> she was taken with strong hysterics i found her kicking and screaming like a good one in strong's chamber along with him and colonel altamont and miss amory crying and as pale as a sheet and altamont fuming about a regular kick up <\s>
<s> they were two hours in the chambers and the old woman went whooping off in a cab <\s>
<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> but it's done and can't be undone and we must make the best of it she has known the story for a month thought pen with a sharp pang of grief and a gloomy sympathy this accounts for her letter of to day <\s>

<s> old bows taught her <\s>

<s> it's what bows says if there were twenty men in a room and one not taking notice of her she wouldn't be satisfied until the twentieth was at her elbow <\s>

<s> pen remembered that blanche had written and mentioned her visit <\s>
<s> i was called in huxter said <\s>
<s> i was in the inn looking after old cos's leg and about something else too very likely and i met strong who told me there was a woman taken ill in chambers and went up to give her my professional services <\s>
<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>
<s> she was taken with strong hysterics i found her kicking and screaming like a good one in strong's chamber along with him and colonel altamont and miss amory crying and as pale as a sheet and altamont fuming about a regular kick up <\s>
<s> they were two hours in the chambers and the old woman went whooping off in a cab <\s>
<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> but it's done and can't be undone and we must make the best of it she has known the story for a month thought pen with a sharp pang of grief and a gloomy sympathy this accounts for her letter of to day <\s>

<s> do you know who altamont is sir <\s>

<s> old bows taught her <\s>
<s> and she'll do on the stage if the governor was to throw me over but i'd rather not have her there <\s>

<s> it's what bows says if there were twenty men in a room and one not taking notice of her she wouldn't be satisfied until the twentieth was at her elbow <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>

<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>

<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>

<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>

<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>

<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>

<s> i was in the inn looking after old cos's leg and about something else too very likely and i met strong who told me there was a woman taken ill in chambers and went up to give her my professional services <\s>
<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>
<s> she was taken with strong hysterics i found her kicking and screaming like a good one in strong's chamber along with him and colonel altamont and miss amory crying and as pale as a sheet and altamont fuming about a regular kick up <\s>
<s> they were two hours in the chambers and the old woman went whooping off in a cab <\s>
<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>
<s> i called in grosvenor place next day to see if i could be of any service but they were gone without so much as thanking me and the day after i had business of my own to attend to a bad business too said mr <\s>
<s> but it's done and can't be undone and we must make the best of it she has known the story for a month thought pen with a sharp pang of grief and a gloomy sympathy this accounts for her letter of to day <\s>
<s> she will not implicate her father or divulge his secret she wishes to let me off from the marriage and finds a pretext the generous girl <\s>
<s> do you know who altamont is sir <\s>
<s> asked huxter after the pause during which pen had been thinking of his own affairs <\s>
<s> fanny and i have talked him over and we can't help fancying that it's mrs <\s>
<s> lightfoot's first husband come to life again and she who has just married a second <\s>

<s> she thinks you can sir said huxter accepting pen's proffered hand and i'm very much obliged to you i'm sure and that you might talk over my father and break the business to him and my mother who always has her back up about being a clergyman's daughter <\s>
<s> fanny ain't of a good family i know and not up to us in breeding and that but she's a huxter now <\s>
<s> the wife takes the husband's rank of course said pen <\s>
<s> and with a little practice in society continued huxter imbibing his stick she'll be as good as any girl in clavering <\s>
<s> you should hear her sing and play on the piano <\s>
<s> old bows taught her <\s>
<s> and she'll do on the stage if the governor was to throw me over but i'd rather not have her there <\s>

<s> i'll be bound to say that two or three of the bartholomew chaps that i've brought into my place are sitting with her now even jack linton that i took down as my best man is as bad as the rest and she will go on singing and making eyes at him <\s>
<s> it's what bows says if there were twenty men in a room and one not taking notice of her she wouldn't be satisfied until the twentieth was at her elbow <\s>

<s> she must keep the lodge <\s>
<s> she can't see so much of her family as she used <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> old bows taught her <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> the wife takes the husband's rank of course said pen <\s>

<s> old bows taught her <\s>
<s> and she'll do on the stage if the governor was to throw me over but i'd rather not have her there <\s>

<s> it's what bows says if there were twenty men in a room and one not taking notice of her she wouldn't be satisfied until the twentieth was at her elbow <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> and she'll do on the stage if the governor was to throw me over but i'd rather not have her there <\s>

<s> it's what bows says if there were twenty men in a room and one not taking notice of her she wouldn't be satisfied until the twentieth was at her elbow <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>
<s> he was thus seated twiddling the queer manuscript in his hand joking grimly to himself when his servant came in with a card from a gentleman who wished to speak to him very particularly <\s>
<s> and if pen had gone out into the passage he would have seen sucking his stick rolling his eyes and showing great marks of anxiety his old acquaintance mr <\s>
<s> huxter on particular business <\s>

<s> pray take a chair mr <\s>

<s> in what way can i be of service to you <\s>

<s> i'm in a fix said mr <\s>

<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>

<s> they were two hours in the chambers and the old woman went whooping off in a cab <\s>
<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>

<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>

<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>

<s> the words of this letter were perfectly clear and written in blanche's neatest hand upon her scented paper and yet the meaning of the composition not a little puzzled pen <\s>
<s> did blanche mean to accept or to refuse his polite offer <\s>
<s> her phrases either meant that pen did not love her and she declined him or that she took him and sacrificed herself to him cold as he was <\s>
<s> he laughed sardonically over the letter and over the transaction which occasioned it <\s>
<s> he laughed to think how fortune had jilted him and how he deserved his slippery fortune <\s>
<s> he turned over and over the musky gilt edged riddle <\s>
<s> it amused his humour he enjoyed it as if it had been a funny story <\s>
<s> he was thus seated twiddling the queer manuscript in his hand joking grimly to himself when his servant came in with a card from a gentleman who wished to speak to him very particularly <\s>
<s> and if pen had gone out into the passage he would have seen sucking his stick rolling his eyes and showing great marks of anxiety his old acquaintance mr <\s>

<s> pray take a chair mr <\s>
<s> huxter said pen in his most superb manner <\s>

<s> i'm in a fix said mr <\s>
<s> she sent me to you continued the young surgeon <\s>

<s> and tell him what <\s>

<s> you you don't mean to say you have you have done any wrong to that dear little creature sir <\s>
<s> said pen starting up in a great fury <\s>
<s> i hope not said huxter with a hangdog look but i've married her <\s>
<s> and i know there will be an awful shindy at home <\s>

<s> it's all over now and the old boy's wrote me that he's coming up to town for drugs he will be here to morrow and then it must all come out <\s>

<s> pen remembered that blanche had written and mentioned her visit <\s>
<s> i was called in huxter said <\s>
<s> i was in the inn looking after old cos's leg and about something else too very likely and i met strong who told me there was a woman taken ill in chambers and went up to give her my professional services <\s>
<s> it was the old lady who attends miss amory her housekeeper or some such thing <\s>
<s> she was taken with strong hysterics i found her kicking and screaming like a good one in strong's chamber along with him and colonel altamont and miss amory crying and as pale as a sheet and altamont fuming about a regular kick up <\s>
<s> they were two hours in the chambers and the old woman went whooping off in a cab <\s>
<s> she was much worse than the young one <\s>
<s> i called in grosvenor place next day to see if i could be of any service but they were gone without so much as thanking me and the day after i had business of my own to attend to a bad business too said mr <\s>
<s> but it's done and can't be undone and we must make the best of it she has known the story for a month thought pen with a sharp pang of grief and a gloomy sympathy this accounts for her letter of to day <\s>
<s> she will not implicate her father or divulge his secret she wishes to let me off from the marriage and finds a pretext the generous girl <\s>
<s> do you know who altamont is sir <\s>
<s> asked huxter after the pause during which pen had been thinking of his own affairs <\s>
<s> fanny and i have talked him over and we can't help fancying that it's mrs <\s>

<s> old bows taught her <\s>
<s> and she'll do on the stage if the governor was to throw me over but i'd rather not have her there <\s>
